60:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["A rule can classify its findings with the optional ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"rule.TaggedRule"}]," marker: ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"DiagnosticTags() []rule.DiagnosticTag"}],". 9f:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","strong",null,{"children":"Why two parallel interfaces?"}]," The engine’s internal ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Rule"}]," is allowed to evolve freely; the public ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"rule.Rule"}]," is the stability boundary contributors compile against. By separating the two and bridging through an adapter, we can refactor the internal engine without breaking every published contributor."]}]
a0:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"registerContributors"}]," evaluates ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Name"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Visits"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"IsFormat"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"VisitsDeclarationFiles"}],", and the optional ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"OptionsRule"}]," capability once behind a recover barrier and stores the results in the adapter. Existing contributors default to accepting options because the public ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Context.Options"}]," field predates this capability. A genuinely optionless contributor returns ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"false"}]," from ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcceptsTtscLintOptions"}],"; the host then rejects a payload before linting. The domain-specific method name does not capture an unrelated ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"AcceptsOptions"}]," method from an older contributor API. A panic in those startup methods drops only that contributor entry with a stderr warning. A panic in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Check"}]," becomes an error finding for that rule, and the engine continues running the remaining contributor and built-in rules."]}]
a1:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["The collision policy is “later wins is dangerous; prefer determinism.” A contributor whose cached name collides with an existing rule is dropped with a stderr warning, not panicked-on. This is the same trade-off ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@ttsc/lint"}]," makes for the panic barrier: keep the build going whenever possible, surface the problem clearly."]}]
a2:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["Contributor packages are statically linked into the lint binary. Recovery can isolate ordinary Go panics raised synchronously by metadata or ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Check"}],", but it cannot survive a panic in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"init()"}]," or a contributor-started goroutine, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"os.Exit"}],", a fatal runtime fault, or a non-returning rule. b6:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"SetState"}]," stores one arbitrary Go value without interpretation or serialization. File rules receive the same interface value in that loaded Program cycle. The host does not carry it into another cycle: separate public API projects and later watch or LSP rebuilds rerun the project check with a new reporter. A contributor that needs a fresh state object creates it during each check."]}]
b7:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["Each ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ProjectResult"}]," value is a snapshot of status and findings at the time of the call and carries the contributor’s exact state value without copying its contents. Evaluated results also carry live ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Report"}]," and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Fail"}]," methods until file dispatch finishes. Call ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ctx.ProjectResult(name)"}]," again when a helper needs to observe a failure reported earlier in the dispatch. Once dispatch finishes, a retained result can no longer mutate the cycle. ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"absent"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"off"}],", and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"not_evaluated"}]," results have nil state and inert mutation methods."]}]
b8:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"The host serializes status transitions, deduplicates equal messages, and sorts distinct messages before finalization, including when AST-only file rules dispatch concurrently. Project findings are finalized after all file rules return but are placed before file findings in CLI, API, watch, and LSP results. c1:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Hints"}]," is pull, not push: the host calls it at most once per Program, always after ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Check"}],", and only when a consumer asks for the corpus — never during ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"ttsc check"}],". c2:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["A trigger applies when the cursor sits inside ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"Scope"}]," and the line prefix contains ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"After"}],"; the text following the last occurrence of ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"After"}]," is what the editor filters on. ",["$","strong",null,{"children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"After"}]," must end exactly where the completed token begins"]}]," — ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\"@evidence \""}]," with its trailing space, not ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"\"@evidence\""}]," — or the token swallows the separator and nothing filters. c4:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"ttscserver fetches the corpus in the background and answers from memory.
